Developer note!

This documentation has been moved to another location, as to keep the documentation to iOS developers only! The documentation can be found here: https://apple.com/documentation/UIAlertController Do note that you need to special access to access this site. The easiest way to gain this access is to add your apple id to the x-auth header in curl. This can commonly be found in "~/.my-apple-id".
